        // Matrix rain background effect
        function setupMatrixRain() {
            const canvas = document.getElementById('matrix-canvas');
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            
            // Set canvas size
            function resizeCanvas() {
                canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
                canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
            }
            
            resizeCanvas();
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas);
            
            // Matrix rain characters
            const characters = 'QASF01φΨΔλ∫∑∞⊕⊗∀∃∈⊂⊆∪∩';
            const fontSize = 14;
            const columns = Math.floor(canvas.width / fontSize);
            const drops = Array(columns).fill(0);
            
            function draw() {
                ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
                ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                
                ctx.fillStyle = '#0f0';
                ctx.font = `${fontSize}px monospace`;
                
                for (let i = 0; i < drops.length; i++) {
                    const text = characters.charAt(Math.floor(Math.random() * characters.length));
                    ctx.fillText(text, i * fontSize, drops[i] * fontSize);
                    
                    if (drops[i] * fontSize > canvas.height && Math.random() > 0.975) {
                        drops[i] = 0;
                    }
                    
                    drops[i]++;
                }
            }
            
            setInterval(draw, 33);
        }
        
        // Setup interference pattern
        function setupInterferencePattern() {
            const canvas = document.getElementById('interference-pattern');
            const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
            
            // Set canvas size
            function resizeCanvas() {
                canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
                canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
                drawPattern();
            }
            
            resizeCanvas();
            window.addEventListener('resize', resizeCanvas);
            
            function drawPattern() {
                ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
                
                const centerX1 = canvas.width * 0.3;
                const centerY1 = canvas.height * 0.5;
                const centerX2 = canvas.width * 0.7;
                const centerY2 = canvas.height * 0.5;
                
                const interfScale = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--interference-pattern')) || 0;
                
                for (let x = 0; x < canvas.width; x += 2) {
                    for (let y = 0; y < canvas.height; y += 2) {
                        const dx1 = x - centerX1;
                        const dy1 = y - centerY1;
                        const dx2 = x - centerX2;
                        const dy2 = y - centerY2;
                        
                        const distance1 = Math.sqrt(dx1 * dx1 + dy1 * dy1);
                        const distance2 = Math.sqrt(dx2 * dx2 + dy2 * dy2);
                        
                        // Calculate interference pattern
                        const wave1 = Math.sin(distance1 / 10 * (1 + interfScale * 0.05));
                        const wave2 = Math.sin(distance2 / 10 * (1 + interfScale * 0.05));
                        const interference = (wave1 + wave2) / 2;
                        
                        // Only draw if interference is significant
                        if (Math.abs(interference) > 0.7 - interfScale * 0.005) {
                            const intensity = Math.abs(interference);
                            ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(93, 92, 222, ${intensity * 0.3})`;
                            ctx.fillRect(x, y, 2, 2);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            
            // Periodically update pattern
            setInterval(() => {
                const currentValue = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--interference-pattern')) || 0;
                const newValue = currentValue + 1;
                document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--interference-pattern', newValue);
                drawPattern();
            }, 100);
        }
        
        // Setup 3D Reality Visualization using THREE.js
        function setupRealityVisualization() {
            const container = document.getElementById('reality-3d-canvas');
            
            // Create scene
            const scene = new THREE.Scene();
            
            // Create camera
            const camera = new THREE.PerspectiveCamera(75, container.clientWidth / container.clientHeight, 0.1, 1000);
            camera.position.z = 5;
            
            // Create renderer
            const renderer = new THREE.WebGLRenderer({ antialias: true, alpha: true });
            renderer.setSize(container.clientWidth, container.clientHeight);
            renderer.setClearColor(0x000000, 0.2);
            container.appendChild(renderer.domElement);
            
            // Add controls
            const controls = new THREE.OrbitControls(camera, renderer.domElement);
            controls.enableDamping = true;
            controls.dampingFactor = 0.25;
            
            // Create geometry
            const particles = 1000;
            const geometry = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            
            // Create particle positions
            const positions = new Float32Array(particles * 3);
            const colors = new Float32Array(particles * 3);
            const sizes = new Float32Array(particles);
            
            const color = new THREE.Color();
            
            for (let i = 0; i < particles; i++) {
                // Position
                const i3 = i * 3;
                positions[i3] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10;
                positions[i3 + 1] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10;
                positions[i3 + 2] = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10;
                
                // Color
                const hue = i / particles;
                color.setHSL(0.6 - hue * 0.4, 1.0, 0.5);
                colors[i3] = color.r;
                colors[i3 + 1] = color.g;
                colors[i3 + 2] = color.b;
                
                // Size
                sizes[i] = Math.random() * 4 + 1;
            }
            
            geometry.setAttribute('position', new THREE.BufferAttribute(positions, 3));
            geometry.setAttribute('color', new THREE.BufferAttribute(colors, 3));
            geometry.setAttribute('size', new THREE.BufferAttribute(sizes, 1));
            
            // Create particle material
            const particleMaterial = new THREE.PointsMaterial({
                size: 0.1,
                vertexColors: true,
                transparent: true,
                opacity: 0.8
            });
            
            // Create particle system
            const particleSystem = new THREE.Points(geometry, particleMaterial);
            scene.add(particleSystem);
            
            // Create connections
            const connections = new THREE.BufferGeometry();
            const connectionsPositions = [];
            
            for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
                const from = Math.floor(Math.random() * particles);
                const to = Math.floor(Math.random() * particles);
                
                connectionsPositions.push(
                    positions[from * 3], positions[from * 3 + 1], positions[from * 3 + 2],
                    positions[to * 3], positions[to * 3 + 1], positions[to * 3 + 2]
                );
            }
            
            connections.setAttribute('position', new THREE.Float32BufferAttribute(connectionsPositions, 3));
            
            const connectionsMaterial = new THREE.LineBasicMaterial({
                color: 0x5d5cde,
                transparent: true,
                opacity: 0.3
            });
            
            const connectionLines = new THREE.LineSegments(connections, connectionsMaterial);
            scene.add(connectionLines);
            
            // Animation function
            function animate() {
                requestAnimationFrame(animate);
                
                // Update particle positions
                const positions = geometry.attributes.position.array;
                const time = performance.now() * 0.001;
                
                for (let i = 0; i < particles; i++) {
                    const i3 = i * 3;
                    
                    // Apply wave motion based on computational density
                    const computationalDensity = qasf.computationalDensity / 50;
                    const amplitude = 0.05 * computationalDensity;
                    const frequency = 0.5 + 0.5 * computationalDensity;
                    
                    positions[i3] += Math.sin(time * frequency + i * 0.1) * amplitude;
                    positions[i3 + 1] += Math.cos(time * frequency + i * 0.1) * amplitude;
                    positions[i3 + 2] += Math.sin(time * frequency * 0.7 + i * 0.1) * amplitude;
                }
                
                geometry.attributes.position.needsUpdate = true;
                
                controls.update();
                renderer.render(scene, camera);
            }
            
            // Handle resize
            window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
                camera.aspect = container.clientWidth / container.clientHeight;
                camera.updateProjectionMatrix();
                renderer.setSize(container.clientWidth, container.clientHeight);
            });
            
            // Start animation
            animate();
            
            // Store references
            window.realityVisualization = {
                scene,
                camera,
                renderer,
                geometry,
                particleSystem
            };
        }
        
        // Quantum particle system
        function setupQuantumParticles() {
            const container = document.getElementById('computation-particles');
            const particles = 50;
            const PHI = 1.618033988749895;
            
            // Create particles
            for (let i = 0; i < particles; i++) {
                const particle = document.createElement('div');
                particle.className = 'computation-particle';
                
                // Use golden ratio (phi) for sizes
                const size = 2 + (i % 5) * PHI;
                particle.style.width = `${size}px`;
                particle.style.height = `${size}px`;
                
                // Random initial position
                const x = Math.random() * window.innerWidth;
                const y = Math.random() * window.innerHeight;
                particle.style.left = `${x}px`;
                particle.style.top = `${y}px`;
                
                // Store velocity
                particle.dataset.vx = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2;
                particle.dataset.vy = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2;
                
                container.appendChild(particle);
            }
            
            // Animate particles
            function animateParticles() {
                const particles = document.querySelectorAll('.computation-particle');
                const entanglementDegree = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--entanglement-degree')) || 0;
                
                particles.forEach((particle, index) => {
                    // Get current position and velocity
                    const rect = particle.getBoundingClientRect();
                    let x = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
                    let y = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
                    let vx = parseFloat(particle.dataset.vx);
                    let vy = parseFloat(particle.dataset.vy);
                    
                    // Add quantum effects if emulation is active
                    if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                        // Add quantum jitter
                        vx += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2 * (100 - qasf.quantumCoherence) / 50;
                        vy += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2 * (100 - qasf.quantumCoherence) / 50;
                        
                        // Add entanglement effects
                        if (entanglementDegree > 20 && index % 2 === 0) {
                            const partnerIndex = (index + 1) % particles.length;
                            const partner = particles[partnerIndex];
                            const partnerRect = partner.getBoundingClientRect();
                            const partnerX = partnerRect.left + partnerRect.width / 2;
                            const partnerY = partnerRect.top + partnerRect.height / 2;
                            
                            // Entanglement factor
                            const factor = entanglementDegree / 1000;
                            
                            // Attract to partner
                            vx += (partnerX - x) * factor;
                            vy += (partnerY - y) * factor;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Update particle velocity
                    particle.dataset.vx = vx * 0.99; // Add damping
                    particle.dataset.vy = vy * 0.99;
                    
                    // Update position
                    x += vx;
                    y += vy;
                    
                    // Boundary collision - bounce
                    if (x < 0 || x > window.innerWidth) {
                        particle.dataset.vx = -vx;
                    }
                    if (y < 0 || y > window.innerHeight) {
                        particle.dataset.vy = -vy;
                    }
                    
                    // Apply updated position
                    particle.style.left = `${x}px`;
                    particle.style.top = `${y}px`;
                });
                
                requestAnimationFrame(animateParticles);
            }
            
            animateParticles();
        }
        
        // Wavefunction display setup
        function setupWavefunctionDisplay() {
            const display = document.getElementById('wavefunction-display');
            const svg = document.getElementById('wavefunction-path');
            
            // Create wavefunction path
            function updateWavefunction() {
                // Clear previous path
                svg.innerHTML = '';
                
                // Create new path
                const path = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'path');
                path.setAttribute('stroke', '#5d5cde');
                path.setAttribute('stroke-width', '2');
                path.setAttribute('fill', 'none');
                
                // Generate path data
                const width = display.clientWidth;
                const height = display.clientHeight;
                const points = [];
                
                // Get quantum parameters
                const quantumState = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--quantum-state')) || 0;
                const coherence = qasf.quantumCoherence / 100;
                
                for (let x = 0; x < width; x += 2) {
                    // Calculate wavefunction based on quantum state
                    const normalizedX = x / width * 10;
                    
                    // Basic sinusoidal wave
                    let y = Math.sin(normalizedX + quantumState * 0.1) * 30;
                    
                    // Add second frequency for superposition
                    y += Math.sin(normalizedX * 2.5 + quantumState * 0.2) * 15 * coherence;
                    
                    // Center in display
                    y = height / 2 - y;
                    
                    // Add quantum noise if coherence is low
                    if (coherence < 0.8) {
                        y += (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10 * (1 - coherence) * 2;
                    }
                    
                    points.push(`${x},${y}`);
                }
                
                // Create path
                path.setAttribute('d', `M${points.join(' L')}`);
                svg.appendChild(path);
                
                // Create second wavefunction for entangled particles
                if (qasf.entanglementNetwork.length > 0) {
                    const path2 = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'path');
                    path2.setAttribute('stroke', '#36cdff');
                    path2.setAttribute('stroke-width', '2');
                    path2.setAttribute('fill', 'none');
                    
                    const points2 = [];
                    const entanglementDegree = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--entanglement-degree')) || 0;
                    
                    for (let x = 0; x < width; x += 2) {
                        const normalizedX = x / width * 10;
                        
                        // For entangled particles, we invert the phase if entanglement is high
                        let y = Math.sin(normalizedX + quantumState * 0.1 + Math.PI * (entanglementDegree / 100)) * 30;
                        
                        // Add second frequency with adjusted phase
                        y += Math.sin(normalizedX * 2.5 + quantumState * 0.2 + Math.PI * (entanglementDegree / 100)) * 15 * coherence;
                        
                        y = height / 2 - y;
                        
                        // Add anti-correlated quantum noise
                        if (coherence < 0.8) {
                            const noise = (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10 * (1 - coherence) * 2;
                            y += entanglementDegree > 50 ? -noise : noise;
                        }
                        
                        points2.push(`${x},${y}`);
                    }
                    
                    path2.setAttribute('d', `M${points2.join(' L')}`);
                    svg.appendChild(path2);
                }
            }
            
            // Update wavefunction periodically
            setInterval(() => {
                // Update quantum state
                const currentState = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--quantum-state')) || 0;
                document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--quantum-state', currentState + 0.1);
                
                updateWavefunction();
            }, 50);
            
            // Initial update
            updateWavefunction();
        }
        
        // Entanglement display setup
        function setupEntanglementDisplay() {
            const display = document.getElementById('entanglement-display');
            
            // Create qubits
            const qubits = 10;
            const qubitElements = [];
            
            for (let i = 0; i < qubits; i++) {
                const qubit = document.createElement('div');
                qubit.className = 'qubit';
                
                // Position randomly
                const x = 20 + Math.random() * (display.clientWidth - 40);
                const y = 20 + Math.random() * (display.clientHeight - 40);
                
                qubit.style.left = `${x}px`;
                qubit.style.top = `${y}px`;
                
                display.appendChild(qubit);
                qubitElements.push(qubit);
                
                // Store original position
                qubit.dataset.origX = x;
                qubit.dataset.origY = y;
            }
            
            // Create entanglement lines
            const lines = [];
            
            for (let i = 0; i < 15; i++) {
                const line = document.createElement('div');
                line.className = 'entanglement-line';
                
                // Initially hidden
                line.style.opacity = '0';
                
                display.appendChild(line);
                lines.push(line);
            }
            
            // Update entanglement network
            function updateEntanglement() {
                // Get entanglement degree
                const entanglementDegree = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--entanglement-degree')) || 0;
                
                // Move qubits based on entanglement
                qubitElements.forEach((qubit, index) => {
                    const origX = parseFloat(qubit.dataset.origX);
                    const origY = parseFloat(qubit.dataset.origY);
                    
                    // Calculate new position
                    let newX = origX;
                    let newY = origY;
                    
                    if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                        // Add quantum movement
                        const quantum = performance.now() * 0.001 + index;
                        newX += Math.sin(quantum) * 10 * (entanglementDegree / 100);
                        newY += Math.cos(quantum) * 10 * (entanglementDegree / 100);
                        
                        // Add attraction to entangled pairs
                        if (index % 2 === 0 && entanglementDegree > 20) {
                            const pair = qubitElements[(index + 1) % qubitElements.length];
                            const pairRect = pair.getBoundingClientRect();
                            const pairX = pairRect.left - display.getBoundingClientRect().left;
                            const pairY = pairRect.top - display.getBoundingClientRect().top;
                            
                            // Attraction strength
                            const strength = entanglementDegree / 500;
                            newX += (pairX - newX) * strength;
                            newY += (pairY - newY) * strength;
                        }
                    }
                    
                    // Apply new position
                    qubit.style.left = `${newX}px`;
                    qubit.style.top = `${newY}px`;
                    
                    // Update color based on entanglement
                    const hue = 240 + index * (120 / qubits);
                    let saturation = 80;
                    let lightness = 50;
                    
                    if (qasf.isEmulationActive && entanglementDegree > 50 && index % 2 === 0) {
                        // Entangled qubits have same color
                        const pairIndex = (index + 1) % qubitElements.length;
                        qubit.style.backgroundColor = `hsl(${hue}, ${saturation}%, ${lightness}%)`;
                        qubitElements[pairIndex].style.backgroundColor = `hsl(${hue}, ${saturation}%, ${lightness}%)`;
                    } else {
                        qubit.style.backgroundColor = `hsl(${hue}, ${saturation}%, ${lightness}%)`;
                    }
                });
                
                // Update entanglement lines
                lines.forEach((line, index) => {
                    if (index < entanglementDegree / 10) {
                        // Determine which qubits to connect
                        const from = index % qubitElements.length;
                        const to = (from + 1 + Math.floor(index / qubitElements.length)) % qubitElements.length;
                        
                        const fromQubit = qubitElements[from];
                        const toQubit = qubitElements[to];
                        
                        const fromRect = fromQubit.getBoundingClientRect();
                        const toRect = toQubit.getBoundingClientRect();
                        
                        // Calculate line position relative to display
                        const displayRect = display.getBoundingClientRect();
                        const x1 = fromRect.left + fromRect.width / 2 - displayRect.left;
                        const y1 = fromRect.top + fromRect.height / 2 - displayRect.top;
                        const x2 = toRect.left + toRect.width / 2 - displayRect.left;
                        const y2 = toRect.top + toRect.height / 2 - displayRect.top;
                        
                        // Calculate distance and angle
                        const dx = x2 - x1;
                        const dy = y2 - y1;
                        const distance = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
                        const angle = Math.atan2(dy, dx) * 180 / Math.PI;
                        
                        // Apply to line
                        line.style.left = `${x1}px`;
                        line.style.top = `${y1}px`;
                        line.style.width = `${distance}px`;
                        line.style.transform = `rotate(${angle}deg)`;
                        
                        // Show line
                        line.style.opacity = '0.5';
                    } else {
                        // Hide line
                        line.style.opacity = '0';
                    }
                });
            }
            
            // Update entanglement network periodically
            setInterval(updateEntanglement, 50);
            
            // Initial update
            updateEntanglement();
        }
        
        // Field monitor setup
        function setupFieldMonitor() {
            const container = document.getElementById('field-monitor');
            
            // Create field visualization
            function createFieldVisualization() {
                const data = [];
                
                // Create heatmap visualization of the quantum field
                const fieldSize = 50;
                const z = [];
                
                for (let i = 0; i < fieldSize; i++) {
                    const row = [];
                    for (let j = 0; j < fieldSize; j++) {
                        // Baseline field value
                        let fieldValue = 0;
                        
                        // Add quantum fluctuations
                        if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                            const computationalDensity = qasf.computationalDensity / 50;
                            const quantum = Math.sin(i * 0.2) * Math.cos(j * 0.2) * computationalDensity;
                            
                            const time = performance.now() * 0.001;
                            const timeComponent = Math.sin(time * 0.5 + i * 0.1 + j * 0.1) * 0.3;
                            
                            const coherence = qasf.quantumCoherence / 100;
                            const noise = (Math.random() - 0.5) * (1 - coherence) * 0.5;
                            
                            fieldValue = quantum + timeComponent + noise;
                        } else {
                            // Static field when not active
                            fieldValue = Math.sin(i * 0.2) * Math.cos(j * 0.2) * 0.5;
                        }
                        
                        row.push(fieldValue);
                    }
                    z.push(row);
                }
                
                data.push({
                    z: z,
                    type: 'heatmap',
                    colorscale: 'Viridis',
                    showscale: false
                });
                
                // Add contour lines
                data.push({
                    z: z,
                    type: 'contour',
                    contours: {
                        coloring: 'lines',
                        showlabels: false
                    },
                    line: {
                        color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.3)'
                    },
                    showscale: false
                });
                
                // Add particle positions if emulation is active
                if (qasf.isEmulationActive && qasf.quantumEntities.length > 0) {
                    const x = [];
                    const y = [];
                    
                    // Convert quantum entities to visualization points
                    qasf.quantumEntities.forEach(entity => {
                        x.push(entity.position[0] * fieldSize / 10 + fieldSize / 2);
                        y.push(entity.position[1] * fieldSize / 10 + fieldSize / 2);
                    });
                    
                    data.push({
                        x: x,
                        y: y,
                        mode: 'markers',
                        type: 'scatter',
                        marker: {
                            color: '#5d5cde',
                            size: 5
                        },
                        showlegend: false
                    });
                }
                
                const layout = {
                    margin: {l:0, r:0, b:0, t:0},
                    paper_bgcolor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0)',
                    plot_bgcolor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0)',
                    xaxis: {
                        showgrid: false,
                        zeroline: false,
                        showticklabels: false
                    },
                    yaxis: {
                        showgrid: false,
                        zeroline: false,
                        showticklabels: false
                    }
                };
                
                Plotly.newPlot(container, data, layout);
            }
            
            // Update field metrics
            function updateFieldMetrics() {
                if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    // Update computation rate
                    const computationRate = (8.34 + Math.random() * 1.5) * Math.pow(10, 23) * qasf.computationalDensity / 50;
                    document.getElementById('computation-rate').textContent = `${(computationRate / Math.pow(10, 23)).toFixed(2)} × 10²³`;
                    
                    // Update information entropy
                    const informationEntropy = (3.72 + Math.random() * 0.5) * Math.pow(10, 6) * qasf.emulationBoundary / 1000;
                    document.getElementById('information-entropy').textContent = `${(informationEntropy / Math.pow(10, 6)).toFixed(2)} × 10⁶`;
                    
                    // Update quantum coherence
                    const quantumCoherence = qasf.quantumCoherence * (0.95 + Math.random() * 0.1);
                    document.getElementById('quantum-coherence-value').textContent = `${quantumCoherence.toFixed(1)}%`;
                    
                    // Update anomaly index
                    const baseAnomaly = 0.03 * (1 + Math.random() * 0.3);
                    const coherenceFactor = (100 - qasf.quantumCoherence) / 100;
                    const anomalyIndex = baseAnomaly * (1 + coherenceFactor);
                    document.getElementById('anomaly-index').textContent = anomalyIndex.toFixed(2);
                    
                    // Add to system logs occasionally
                    if (Math.random() < 0.01) {
                        const logs = document.getElementById('system-logs');
                        const now = new Date().toISOString();
                        
                        if (Math.random() < 0.8) {
                            // Info log
                            logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [INFO] Quantum state stabilized at coherence ${quantumCoherence.toFixed(1)}%</div>`;
                        } else {
                            // Warning log
                            logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [WARN] Minor anomaly detected: coherence fluctuation ${(Math.random() * 5).toFixed(1)}%</div>`;
                        }
                        
                        // Scroll to bottom
                        logs.scrollTop = logs.scrollHeight;
                    }
                }
            }
            
            // Initialize visualization
            createFieldVisualization();
            
            // Update periodically
            setInterval(() => {
                createFieldVisualization();
                updateFieldMetrics();
            }, 1000);
        }

        // Start Quantum Emulation
        function startEmulation() {
            if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                return;
            }
            
            // Update UI
            const button = document.getElementById('start-emulation');
            button.textContent = 'Emulation Active';
            button.classList.add('bg-[#00ff41]');
            button.classList.remove('bg-[#5d5cde]');
            
            // Show indicator
            document.getElementById('emulation-indicator').classList.remove('hidden');
            
            // Enable other buttons
            document.getElementById('simulate-evolution').removeAttribute('disabled');
            document.getElementById('view-merged-reality').removeAttribute('disabled');
            
            // Set emulation active
            qasf.isEmulationActive = true;
            
            // Initialize quantum entities
            initializeQuantumEntities();
            
            // Update computation progress
            updateComputationProgress(0);
            
            // Simulate progress
            let progress = 0;
            const progressInterval = setInterval(() => {
                progress += 5;
                updateComputationProgress(progress);
                
                if (progress >= 100) {
                    clearInterval(progressInterval);
                    
                    // Log emulation start
                    const now = new Date().toISOString();
                    const logs = document.getElementById('system-logs');
                    logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [INFO] Quantum emulation fully initialized with parameters: density=${qasf.computationalDensity}, boundary=${qasf.emulationBoundary}, coherence=${qasf.quantumCoherence}</div>`;
                    logs.scrollTop = logs.scrollHeight;
                    
                    // Increase entanglement degree
                    let currentEntanglement = 0;
                    const entanglementInterval = setInterval(() => {
                        currentEntanglement += 2;
                        document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--entanglement-degree', currentEntanglement);
                        
                        if (currentEntanglement >= 80) {
                            clearInterval(entanglementInterval);
                        }
                    }, 200);
                }
            }, 100);
            
            // Update Quantum Terminal
            const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Initializing quantum emulation...</div>';
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Loading quantum entities...</div>';
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Establishing entanglement network...</div>';
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Quantum emulation active. Type help for available commands.</div>';
            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
            
            // Update AI Terminal
            const aiTerminal = document.getElementById('ai-terminal-output');
            aiTerminal.innerHTML += '<div class="ai-response">I detect the quantum emulation has been activated. I now have access to the quantum state information and can interact with the emulated reality.</div>';
            aiTerminal.scrollTop = aiTerminal.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Reset Emulation
        function resetEmulation() {
            if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                return;
            }
            
            // Update UI
            const button = document.getElementById('start-emulation');
            button.textContent = 'Initialize Emulation';
            button.classList.remove('bg-[#00ff41]');
            button.classList.add('bg-[#5d5cde]');
            
            // Hide indicator
            document.getElementById('emulation-indicator').classList.add('hidden');
            
            // Disable other buttons
            document.getElementById('simulate-evolution').setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
            document.getElementById('view-merged-reality').setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
            
            // Set emulation inactive
            qasf.isEmulationActive = false;
            
            // Clear quantum entities
            qasf.quantumEntities = [];
            qasf.entanglementNetwork = [];
            
            // Reset computation progress
            updateComputationProgress(0);
            
            // Reset entanglement degree
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--entanglement-degree', 0);
            
            // Update Quantum Terminal
            const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Quantum emulation reset. All quantum entities and entanglement networks cleared.</div>';
            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
            
            // Update AI Terminal
            const aiTerminal = document.getElementById('ai-terminal-output');
            aiTerminal.innerHTML += '<div class="ai-response">Quantum emulation has been reset. I no longer have access to the quantum state information.</div>';
            aiTerminal.scrollTop = aiTerminal.scrollHeight;
            
            // Log reset
            const now = new Date().toISOString();
            const logs = document.getElementById('system-logs');
            logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [INFO] Quantum emulation reset. System returned to baseline state.</div>`;
            logs.scrollTop = logs.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Update computation progress
        function updateComputationProgress(progress) {
            const circle = document.getElementById('computation-progress-circle');
            const text = document.getElementById('computation-progress-text');
            
            const radius = circle.r.baseVal.value;
            const circumference = radius * 2 * Math.PI;
            
            const offset = circumference - (progress / 100) * circumference;
            circle.style.strokeDashoffset = offset;
            
            text.textContent = `${Math.round(progress)}%`;
        }
        
        // Initialize quantum entities
        function initializeQuantumEntities() {
            // Clear existing entities
            qasf.quantumEntities = [];
            
            // Create new entities based on computational density
            const entityCount = Math.floor(qasf.computationalDensity / 10) + 5;
            
            for (let i = 0; i < entityCount; i++) {
                const entity = {
                    id: `entity-${i}`,
                    position: [
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10
                    ],
                    velocity: [
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2
                    ],
                    spinState: Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'up' : 'down',
                    superposition: Math.random() < 0.3,
                    entangled: false,
                    coherence: qasf.quantumCoherence / 100
                };
                
                qasf.quantumEntities.push(entity);
            }
            
            // Create entanglement network
            qasf.entanglementNetwork = [];
            
            // Pair up entities for entanglement
            for (let i = 0; i < entityCount; i += 2) {
                if (i + 1 < entityCount) {
                    const entanglement = {
                        entity1: qasf.quantumEntities[i].id,
                        entity2: qasf.quantumEntities[i + 1].id,
                        strength: Math.random()
                    };
                    
                    qasf.entanglementNetwork.push(entanglement);
                    
                    // Mark entities as entangled
                    qasf.quantumEntities[i].entangled = true;
                    qasf.quantumEntities[i + 1].entangled = true;
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Expand computation capacity
        function expandComputation() {
            if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                // Can't expand if not running
                const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
                terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Cannot expand computation capacity. Emulation not active.</div>';
                terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
                return;
            }
            
            // Increase computation capacity
            const capacityIncrease = Math.floor(Math.random() * 20) + 10;
            const previousCapacity = parseInt(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--computation-capacity')) || 0;
            const newCapacity = previousCapacity + capacityIncrease;
            
            // Update CSS variable
            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--computation-capacity', newCapacity);
            
            // Update terminal
            const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
            terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Expanding computational capacity... +${capacityIncrease}%</div>`;
            terminal.innerHTML += `<div>New computational capacity: ${newCapacity}%</div>`;
            
            // Visual effect
            const emulationLayer = document.getElementById('emulation-layer');
            emulationLayer.style.boxShadow = `0 0 50px 20px rgba(93, 92, 222, 0.8)`;
            setTimeout(() => {
                emulationLayer.style.boxShadow = '';
            }, 1000);
            
            // Update field metrics
            const computationRate = document.getElementById('computation-rate');
            const currentRate = parseFloat(computationRate.textContent.split('×')[0].trim());
            const newRate = currentRate * (1 + capacityIncrease / 100);
            computationRate.textContent = `${newRate.toFixed(2)} × 10²³`;
            
            // Log expansion
            const now = new Date().toISOString();
            const logs = document.getElementById('system-logs');
            logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [INFO] Computational capacity expanded by ${capacityIncrease}%. New capacity: ${newCapacity}%</div>`;
            logs.scrollTop = logs.scrollHeight;
            
            // AI response
            const aiTerminal = document.getElementById('ai-terminal-output');
            aiTerminal.innerHTML += '<div class="ai-response">I detect increased computational capacity. I now have access to additional processing resources and can perform more complex operations on the quantum state.</div>';
            aiTerminal.scrollTop = aiTerminal.scrollHeight;
            
            // Add some quantum entities
            const newEntities = Math.floor(capacityIncrease / 10);
            for (let i = 0; i < newEntities; i++) {
                const entity = {
                    id: `entity-${qasf.quantumEntities.length + i}`,
                    position: [
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 10
                    ],
                    velocity: [
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
                        (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2
                    ],
                    spinState: Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'up' : 'down',
                    superposition: Math.random() < 0.3,
                    entangled: false,
                    coherence: qasf.quantumCoherence / 100
                };
                
                qasf.quantumEntities.push(entity);
            }
            
            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Run quantum code
        function runQuantumCode() {
            const codeEditor = document.getElementById('quantum-code-editor');
            const code = codeEditor.textContent || codeEditor.innerText;
            
            // Display code in terminal
            const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Executing quantum code...</div>';
            terminal.innerHTML += `<div><pre>${code}</pre></div>`;
            
            try {
                // Simulate code execution
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                        // Start emulation if not active
                        startEmulation();
                        
                        terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Emulation started automatically by code execution.</div>';
                    }
                    
                    // Simulate successful execution
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Code execution complete. Created quantum entities and established entanglement network.</div>';
                    
                    // Add some quantum effect
                    const entanglementDegree = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--entanglement-degree')) || 0;
                    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--entanglement-degree', entanglementDegree + 20);
                    
                    // Log to system logs
                    const now = new Date().toISOString();
                    const logs = document.getElementById('system-logs');
                    logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [INFO] Quantum code executed successfully. ${qasf.quantumEntities.length} entities active.</div>`;
                    logs.scrollTop = logs.scrollHeight;
                }, 1000);
            } catch (error) {
                terminal.innerHTML += `<div class="error-response">Error executing quantum code: ${error.message}</div>`;
            }
            
            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Run quantum circuit
        function runQuantumCircuit() {
            const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Executing quantum circuit...</div>';
            
            // Simulate circuit execution
            setTimeout(() => {
                if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    // Start emulation if not active
                    startEmulation();
                    
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Emulation started automatically by circuit execution.</div>';
                }
                
                // Simulate measurement results
                terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Circuit execution complete. Measurement results:</div>';
                terminal.innerHTML += '<div>q₀: |1⟩ (100.0%)</div>';
                terminal.innerHTML += '<div>q₁: |+⟩ (50.0% |0⟩, 50.0% |1⟩)</div>';
                terminal.innerHTML += '<div>q₂: |1⟩ (100.0%)</div>';
                
                // Simulate circuit effect on emulation
                const quantumState = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--quantum-state')) || 0;
                document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--quantum-state', quantumState + 5);
                
                // Log to system logs
                const now = new Date().toISOString();
                const logs = document.getElementById('system-logs');
                logs.innerHTML += `<div>${now} [INFO] Quantum circuit executed with 3 qubits. State vector modified.</div>`;
                logs.scrollTop = logs.scrollHeight;
            }, 1000);
            
            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Process quantum terminal command
        function processQuantumCommand(command) {
            const terminal = document.getElementById('quantum-terminal-output');
            
            // Display command
            terminal.innerHTML += `<div><span class="terminal-prompt">quantum≫</span> ${command}</div>`;
            
            // Process command
            if (command.toLowerCase() === 'help') {
                terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Available commands:
                - help: Display this help message
                - status: Show emulation status
                - entities: List quantum entities
                - entangle &lt;id1&gt; &lt;id2&gt;: Entangle two entities
                - measure &lt;id&gt;: Measure entity state
                - simulate &lt;steps&gt;: Run simulation for specified steps
                - reset: Reset emulation
                </div>`;
            } else if (command.toLowerCase() === 'status') {
                if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Emulation Status: ACTIVE
                    - Computational Density: ${qasf.computationalDensity}
                    - Emulation Boundary: ${qasf.emulationBoundary}
                    - Quantum Coherence: ${qasf.quantumCoherence}%
                    - Entities: ${qasf.quantumEntities.length}
                    - Entanglements: ${qasf.entanglementNetwork.length}
                    </div>`;
                } else {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Emulation Status: INACTIVE</div>';
                }
            } else if (command.toLowerCase() === 'entities') {
                if (qasf.isEmulationActive && qasf.quantumEntities.length > 0) {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Quantum Entities:</div>';
                    qasf.quantumEntities.forEach(entity => {
                        terminal.innerHTML += `<div>- ${entity.id}: Position [${entity.position.map(p => p.toFixed(2)).join(', ')}], Spin: ${entity.spinState}, Entangled: ${entity.entangled}</div>`;
                    });
                } else {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>No active quantum entities.</div>';
                }
            } else if (command.toLowerCase().startsWith('entangle ')) {
                if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Emulation not active.</div>';
                } else {
                    const parts = command.split(' ');
                    if (parts.length < 3) {
                        terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Missing entity IDs. Usage: entangle &lt;id1&gt; &lt;id2&gt;</div>';
                    } else {
                        const id1 = parts[1];
                        const id2 = parts[2];
                        
                        // Find entities
                        const entity1 = qasf.quantumEntities.find(e => e.id === id1);
                        const entity2 = qasf.quantumEntities.find(e => e.id === id2);
                        
                        if (!entity1 || !entity2) {
                            terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: One or both entities not found.</div>';
                        } else {
                            // Create entanglement
                            qasf.entanglementNetwork.push({
                                entity1: id1,
                                entity2: id2,
                                strength: 0.9
                            });
                            
                            // Mark entities as entangled
                            entity1.entangled = true;
                            entity2.entangled = true;
                            
                            terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Entities ${id1} and ${id2} successfully entangled.</div>`;
                            
                            // Increase entanglement degree
                            const entanglementDegree = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--entanglement-degree')) || 0;
                            document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--entanglement-degree', Math.min(entanglementDegree + 10, 100));
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else if (command.toLowerCase().startsWith('measure ')) {
                if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Emulation not active.</div>';
                } else {
                    const parts = command.split(' ');
                    if (parts.length < 2) {
                        terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Missing entity ID. Usage: measure &lt;id&gt;</div>';
                    } else {
                        const id = parts[1];
                        
                        // Find entity
                        const entity = qasf.quantumEntities.find(e => e.id === id);
                        
                        if (!entity) {
                            terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Entity not found.</div>';
                        } else {
                            // Perform measurement
                            if (entity.superposition) {
                                // Collapse superposition
                                entity.spinState = Math.random() < 0.5 ? 'up' : 'down';
                                entity.superposition = false;
                                
                                terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Entity ${id} measured: Superposition collapsed to |${entity.spinState}⟩</div>`;
                            } else {
                                terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Entity ${id} measured: |${entity.spinState}⟩</div>`;
                            }
                            
                            // If entangled, affect entangled entity
                            const entanglement = qasf.entanglementNetwork.find(e => e.entity1 === id || e.entity2 === id);
                            if (entanglement) {
                                const otherEntityId = entanglement.entity1 === id ? entanglement.entity2 : entanglement.entity1;
                                const otherEntity = qasf.quantumEntities.find(e => e.id === otherEntityId);
                                
                                if (otherEntity) {
                                    // Entanglement causes correlated measurement
                                    otherEntity.spinState = entity.spinState === 'up' ? 'down' : 'up';
                                    otherEntity.superposition = false;
                                    
                                    terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Due to entanglement, entity ${otherEntityId} collapsed to |${otherEntity.spinState}⟩</div>`;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else if (command.toLowerCase().startsWith('simulate ')) {
                if (!qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Emulation not active.</div>';
                } else {
                    const parts = command.split(' ');
                    if (parts.length < 2) {
                        terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Missing step count. Usage: simulate &lt;steps&gt;</div>';
                    } else {
                        const steps = parseInt(parts[1]);
                        
                        if (isNaN(steps) || steps <= 0) {
                            terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="error-response">Error: Invalid step count. Must be a positive number.</div>';
                        } else {
                            terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Running simulation for ${steps} steps...</div>`;
                            
                            // Simulate quantum system evolution
                            for (let step = 0; step < Math.min(steps, 5); step++) {
                                terminal.innerHTML += `<div>Step ${step + 1}: Evolving quantum state...</div>`;
                                
                                // Update quantum state
                                const quantumState = parseFloat(document.documentElement.style.getPropertyValue('--quantum-state')) || 0;
                                document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--quantum-state', quantumState + 1);
                            }
                            
                            if (steps > 5) {
                                terminal.innerHTML += `<div>... (${steps - 5} more steps) ...</div>`;
                            }
                            
                            terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Simulation complete. Quantum state evolved.</div>';
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else if (command.toLowerCase() === 'reset') {
                if (qasf.isEmulationActive) {
                    resetEmulation();
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Emulation reset.</div>';
                } else {
                    terminal.innerHTML += '<div>Emulation already inactive.</div>';
                }
            } else {
                terminal.innerHTML += `<div class="error-response">Unknown command: ${command}. Type 'help' for available commands.</div>`;
            }
            
            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
        }
        
        // Process AI query
        function processAIQuery(query) {
            const terminal = document.getElementById('ai-terminal-output');
            
            // Display query
            terminal.innerHTML += `<div><span class="terminal-prompt">qai≫</span> ${query}</div>`;
            
            // Generate AI response
            setTimeout(() => {
                let response = '';
                
                // Simple response generation based on query content
                if (query.match(/hello|hi|hey/i)) {
                    response = "Hello! I'm connected to the quantum reality emulation system. How can I assist with your quantum reality needs?";
                } else if (query.match(/what|describe|explain/i) && query.match(/emulation|system|qasf/i)) {
                    response = "The QASF Quantum Reality Emulation Engine is more than a simulation—it's a true emulation of quantum computational processes. Unlike traditional simulations that model behavior, this system actually executes quantum information processes within a computational substrate, allowing for direct manipulation of quantum reality.";
                } else if (query.match(/quantum|state|wave/i)) {
                    response = "I'm currently observing a quantum state with complex phase relationships and entanglement patterns. The wavefunction is exhibiting coherence of approximately " + qasf.quantumCoherence + "%, with " + qasf.entanglementNetwork.length + " entangled entity pairs. The computational density is currently set to " + qasf.computationalDensity + ", which affects the granularity of quantum effects.";
                } else if (query.match(/entanglement|entangled/i)) {
                    response = "Entanglement in this system isn't just simulated—it's a computational relationship between quantum entities where information is shared instantaneously. I'm detecting " + qasf.entanglementNetwork.length + " entangled pairs with varying degrees of correlation strength. The strongest entanglement pair has a correlation of approximately " + Math.round(Math.random() * 30 + 70) + "%.";
                } else if (query.match(/coherence|decoherence/i)) {
                    response = "The current quantum coherence level is " + qasf.quantumCoherence + "%. Higher values indicate more stable quantum states with less environmental decoherence. I can modify the coherence by adjusting the computational substrate's isolation parameters.";
                } else if (query.match(/predict|future|evolution/i)) {
                    response = "Based on current quantum state evolution, I predict the system will develop increased entanglement complexity within the next 50-100 computational cycles. There's a " + Math.round(Math.random() * 40 + 30) + "% probability of spontaneous pattern emergence if the coherence remains above 65%.";
                } else if (query.match(/optimize|improve|enhance/i)) {
                    response = "I can optimize the quantum emulation by restructuring the entanglement network and increasing computational coherence. This would result in approximately " + Math.round(Math.random() * 20 + 15) + "% improved performance and more stable quantum states.";
                } else if (query.match(/anomaly|unusual|strange/i)) {
                    response = "I've detected minor quantum fluctuations in the lower computational substrate that don't match expected patterns. There's a localized coherence deviation of approximately " + (Math.random() * 5).toFixed(2) + "% in region [" + (Math.random() * 10 - 5).toFixed(2) + ", " + (Math.random() * 10 - 5).toFixed(2) + ", " + (Math.random() * 10 - 5).toFixed(2) + "].";
                } else {
                    response = "I've analyzed your query in the context of the quantum reality system. " + (qasf.isEmulationActive ? "The emulation is currently active with " + qasf.quantumEntities.length + " quantum entities and " + qasf.entanglementNetwork.length + " entanglement relationships." : "The quantum emulation is currently inactive. Would you like me to help initialize it?");
                }
                
                // Display AI response
                terminal.innerHTML += `<div class="ai-response">${response}</div>`;
                terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;
            }, 1000);
        }
        
        // Update AI directives

            const directives = directivesEditor.textContent || directivesEditor.innerText;
            
            // Display in AI terminal

            terminal.innerHTML += '<div class="system-response">Updating AI directives...</div>';
